msg:Because Baoding is too close to Beijing, every time I travel, I don’t have many opportunities to stay in Baoding. I spend more than half of the time staying in hotels outside. Starlight’s service and quality are definitely among the best. This time I stayed here, let me appreciate Baoding’s hotel services and services. The quality is impressive, and you can come to Starlight often in the future. I don’t like writing reviews very much. I have written so much this time, please read slowly😂

The location of the hotel is absolutely convenient. Baobai Shopping Center is opposite. Walk 500 meters to the left to see the North Country. There is donkey meat Cao at 1200 meters. There are many popular restaurants around, and it is convenient to go to various attractions.

When booking a room, after placing the order, the hotel quickly called to confirm and confirm according to my remarks, and asked whether to drive, the approximate time to arrive at the hotel and the license plate number, and informed that a parking space would be reserved. It's not very special here, because there are some hotels like this. When we arrived at the hotel, we realized that the phone call from the hotel was not just a question, but was carried out by every hotel staff very seriously. Special thanks to the girl who called. She took the trouble and called several times to inform me that I missed some options when I made the reservation and dealt with my needs very well.

Arrived at the entrance of the hotel parking lot, the master of the parking lot was about to ask us, suddenly I found a strong light in his eyes, as if to say, but when you came, he did not continue to ask, but put it at the entrance The cone moved away, waved to us, and signaled us to follow him, while the master led the way and guided us to a very good reserved parking space with a cone. I was shocked at that time👍. The hotel's parking lot is very large, and parking is very convenient.

The same is true when you enter the hotel to go through the formalities. The front desk will tell you what your needs are and how we can help you arrange them, which is very detailed.

The complimentary afternoon tea is a small snack and a cup of hot drink, which is received at the bakery left by Block B, which is very good.

The hotel provides daily fruits, hot milk before going to bed, and small snacks, which is very considerate.

The breakfast in the hotel is very good. There are special Baoding donkey fire and beef pancakes. There are also fried dough sticks, tofu nao and porridge. There are many varieties. There are prawns for breakfast on the first day😂

Besides, the hardware of the hotel is of good quality, the room is spacious, clean and comfortable, the layout is reasonable, the bathroom is large, the location of the bathtub and sink is well designed, and the air conditioner in the room is very warm and quiet, very good, yes, Also, there is a big word on the small refrigerator in the room that you can enjoy it for free, that is, the drinks and beer in the small refrigerator are free.

All in all, a very satisfying stay👍

msg:酒店是保定少有的五星酒店在市區，而且位置非常方便，挨着朝陽大街，對面就是保定百貨，附近吃喝玩樂比較多也比較熱鬧。
酒店的房間分為A區和B區，B區是酒店老樓，A區是新樓，通過一樓前台聯通。B區房間非常舊，但房間面積相對大一些，不過年輕人住慣了五星酒店，肯定是很難接受B區房間。
酒店給升級為A區房間，這個舉措體現了對客人的重視，很加分，雖然中間的一位服務員在帶我們看房間時比較沒耐心，總以沒有可比較房間為理由想打發我們，但好在前台先後兩位男生客服，都比較負責，真心誠意給客人解決問題，而不是找藉口搪塞，體現了客服人員的敬業度。五分好評給到他們。

posted:Posted July 4, 2021
msg:保定不是個旅遊城市，市區酒店就能看出來，基本上酒店設施老舊，但是這家應該是保定市區條件最高的酒店了。隔壁就是另外一家五星，但是明顯商務會議更多，這裏大部分都是住店的，相對安靜，不像隔壁那麼嘈雜。酒店內部一看就是老字號五星酒店了，硬件不錯，但是一看就是比較有歷史那種。服務態度非常好，不像老字號那樣。酒店早餐很好，可以和北京上海比比。酒店內部也有淮揚菜、日料、自助餐，自助餐298買一送一。離店的時候，店家贈送了端午禮盒，不得不説，這次保定之行，驢肉和星光國際加分不少，保定市區強力推薦，沒有之一。

posted:Posted June 24, 2021
msg:酒店位置很好，處於保定核心地帶，周圍餐飲和購物都很方便，馬路對面就是保定最好的保百購物廣場。早餐也不錯。酒店裡的小冰箱還有免費飲料。建議酒店把桌子上放的小冰箱裏的免費飲料的提示牌的字搞大一些，讓人一眼看清。既然免費，為什麼不更明白地告訴客人呢。另外，酒店僅游泳池開放，健身房不開。建議酒店考慮開放健身房，一些客人是需要健身的。同期保定其它酒店的健身房是開的，説明可以辦到的。
